## Page 3

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:29.88pt;color:#000000">岖</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:18.60pt;color:#000000">CH</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:27.28pt;color:#000000">而</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:18.71pt;color:#000000">TES</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.26pt;color:#000000">高可用架构是一个关注</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.15pt;color:#000000">E</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.02pt;color:#000000">联网架构前沿及高可用、</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.57pt;color:#000000">可扩展及高性能领域知识传播的技术社区</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:3.65pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.33pt;color:#000000">旨在</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.04pt;color:#000000">为</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.39pt;color:#000000">E</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.58pt;color:#000000">联网及软件系统架构师提供一个高效的交流</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.04pt;color:#000000">学习平台。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.25pt;color:#000000">高可用架构性区一直秉承“分享＋交流”的精神，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.57pt;color:#000000">提倡入人参与，以让更多人从社区获得高质量的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.33pt;color:#000000">内窑</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.97pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.57pt;color:#000000">社群由数万名来自国内外亘联网行业的首</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.97pt;color:#000000">席架构师、</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.34pt;color:#000000">CTO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.47pt;color:#000000"> 、技术专家等群体组成，是业界</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.35pt;color:#000000">从业人员学习</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.26pt;color:#000000">E</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.45pt;color:#000000">联网架向及了解架构动态的合适</span>

## Page 5

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.30pt;color:#000000">内容简介</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.57pt;color:#000000">本书由数十位一线架构师的实践与经验凝结而成，选材兼顾技术性、前瞻性与专业深度。各技术焦</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.81pt;color:#000000">点，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.36pt;color:#000000">均由极具代表性的领域专家或实践先行者撰文深度剖析，共同组成“高可用”的全局视野与领先高度，内</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.27pt;color:#000000">容包括精华案例、分布式原理、电商架构等热门专题，及云计算、容器、运维、大数据、安全等重点方向。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.29pt;color:#000000">不仅架构师可以从中受益，其他</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.60pt;color:#000000">IT</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.12pt;color:#000000">、互联网技术从业者同样可以得到提升。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.21pt;color:#000000">未经许可，不得以任何方式复制或抄袭本书之部分或全部内容。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.04pt;color:#000000">版权所有，侵权必究。</span>

## Page 6

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:18.94pt;color:#000000">推</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:19.22pt;color:#000000">荐序</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:10.60pt;color:#000000">1</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:19.72pt;color:#000000">技术没有高低</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.23pt;color:#000000">高</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.56pt;color:#000000">可用架构居然成书了，厚厚的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.35pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.59pt;color:#000000">本，让人赞叹。从</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.00pt;color:#000000">Tim</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.89pt;color:#000000">Yang</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.62pt;color:#000000"> 建立这个社群开始，我</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.36pt;color:#000000">就一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.64pt;color:#000000">直参与其</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.59pt;color:#000000">中，然而</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.36pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.77pt;color:#000000">切发生得如此之快，如此之自然，出乎我的意料。我想，这也是</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.42pt;color:#000000">侠少约</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.54pt;color:#000000">我写序的原因之</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.23pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">吧</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.06pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.68pt;color:#000000">这本书的作者里有太多</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.76pt;color:#000000">我熟悉的朋友，确切地说，我跟他们中的大多数人都是很好的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.40pt;color:#000000">朋友</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.06pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.49pt;color:#000000">他们都乐</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.60pt;color:#000000">于将自己的所知所学分享给社区</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.62pt;color:#000000">，而我也每每从他们那里学到各种技术知</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.75pt;color:#000000">识。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.43pt;color:#000000">你可能会惊讶于本书</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.49pt;color:#000000">内容的跨度之大，从业务系统到数据库，从容器到安全，从社区</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.64pt;color:#000000">建设到行</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.77pt;color:#000000">业观察，包罗万象。同时，讲解内容又实实在在，没有很多空话，偶有没说清楚</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.35pt;color:#000000">的地方</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.13pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.52pt;color:#000000">肯定会有</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.39pt;color:#000000">问</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.55pt;color:#000000">答环节来</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.49pt;color:#000000">补充说明</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.06pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.63pt;color:#000000">因为都是群内昕讲的人提问，所以问答也非常契</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.76pt;color:#000000">合主题。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.36pt;color:#000000">这就保证了本书在特定章节上，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.61pt;color:#000000">比大多数同类书要讲得透彻、明白，适合初级人员阅</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.32pt;color:#000000">读。同</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.62pt;color:#000000">时，对中高级技术人员又有更大的价值。我们经常说架构师对技术的把握要有深度，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.53pt;color:#000000">也要有广度。广度</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.63pt;color:#000000">从何而来？只能是读万卷书、阅千套系统积累而来。本书无疑是</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.23pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.57pt;color:#000000">个很</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.46pt;color:#000000">好的素材源</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.93pt;color:#000000">泉。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">具</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.50pt;color:#000000">体内容在此不赘述，相信大家仔细阅读后会收获颇丰。这里我还是介绍一下背后的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.53pt;color:#000000">这群</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.66pt;color:#000000">人一一这个由分享者和昕众共同组成的大群体，这个被称为高可用架构群的组织。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.58pt;color:#000000">我经常讲，高可用架构这</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.54pt;color:#000000">个群，像极了</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.19pt;color:#000000">《一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.35pt;color:#000000">代</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.12pt;color:#000000">宗</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.61pt;color:#000000">师》里的金楼</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.06pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.60pt;color:#000000">因为你仔细看，技术</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.59pt;color:#000000">圈就像是互联</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.63pt;color:#000000">网时代的武林</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.51pt;color:#000000">。大家</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.78pt;color:#000000">聚在这里，是因为在自己的领域里有所建树，都身怀绝</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.39pt;color:#000000">技面对这</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.37pt;color:#000000">个世界</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.99pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.51pt;color:#000000">所以我们会看到骄傲和拼搏，也会看到争论。因为很多人也都想着，功</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.22pt;color:#000000">夫是</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.22pt;color:#000000">横</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.44pt;color:#000000">坚，站着的才有资格说话</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.37pt;color:#000000">，错的，躺下</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.19pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.02pt;color:#000000">但幸运的是，</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">他们找到了</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.35pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.64pt;color:#000000">种方式来平息这种内心的躁动，就是通过在群里进行分</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.46pt;color:#000000">享</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.46pt;color:#000000">和答疑</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.20pt;color:#000000">来进行“比武”</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.06pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.58pt;color:#000000">你说你的方式可行，那就来分享吧。只要你的话我能懂，只要你的</span>

## Page 7

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.91pt;color:#000000">高可用架构（第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.61pt;color:#000000">1</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.74pt;color:#000000"> 卷）</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.49pt;color:#000000">回答能使我满意，我便服气。而且慢慢地，大家也都认可了这种</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.33pt;color:#000000">方式</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.32pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.02pt;color:#000000">技术领域之宽广，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.59pt;color:#000000">并非</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.36pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.76pt;color:#000000">个人可以统领。而承认</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.47pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">个人在某</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.47pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">个领域比你强并不</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.36pt;color:#000000">丢</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.76pt;color:#000000">人，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.63pt;color:#000000">并不意</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.24pt;color:#000000">味</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.47pt;color:#000000">着</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.36pt;color:#000000">你</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.55pt;color:#000000">不可以</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.36pt;color:#000000">在另外的领域独领风骚。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.61pt;color:#000000">随着时间的流逝，这种由技术驱动的交流也慢慢发酵成了</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.40pt;color:#000000">真正</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.76pt;color:#000000">的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.56pt;color:#000000">友情。金楼戏里最让</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.36pt;color:#000000">“</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.35pt;color:#000000"> 八</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.46pt;color:#000000">卦手黑</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.13pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.29pt;color:#000000">小心！”</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.57pt;color:#000000">账房说</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.13pt;color:#000000">：</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.44pt;color:#000000">“形意拳霸道，千万别轻敌</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.13pt;color:#000000">！</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.39pt;color:#000000">”勇哥说：“追风赶月别留情，你</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.46pt;color:#000000">一定得</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.43pt;color:#000000">响啊！</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.19pt;color:#000000">”</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.62pt;color:#000000">期待从群里接收来自各方的审</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.23pt;color:#000000">言</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.06pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.22pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.39pt;color:#000000">群所学为</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.27pt;color:#000000">人学，</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.90pt;color:#000000">这种健康的氛围在技术圈里也愈发变得可贵</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.19pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.60pt;color:#000000">现在</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.67pt;color:#000000">互联网</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.71pt;color:#000000">在</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.77pt;color:#000000">迅猛</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.71pt;color:#000000">发展</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.54pt;color:#000000">，很</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.99pt;color:#000000">多</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">新</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.56pt;color:#000000">的技术</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.78pt;color:#000000">被发明和引入了进来，碰撞和争论在所难免</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.12pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.64pt;color:#000000">但有</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.36pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.47pt;color:#000000">些圈</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.36pt;color:#000000">子</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.59pt;color:#000000">却变</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.47pt;color:#000000">得</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.02pt;color:#000000">特别吵闹，</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.61pt;color:#000000">为了一个框</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.63pt;color:#000000">高可用架构的这群人，都是工作在各个公</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.64pt;color:#000000">司</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.76pt;color:#000000">的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.23pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.54pt;color:#000000">线技术</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.46pt;color:#000000">管理人</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.64pt;color:#000000">员</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.38pt;color:#000000">，</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.23pt;color:#000000">工</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.61pt;color:#000000">程技术</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.06pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.64pt;color:#000000">但其实他们也很普通，跟你一样，每</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.35pt;color:#000000">天都在</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.54pt;color:#000000">默默地</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.23pt;color:#000000">工</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.35pt;color:#000000">作和</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.53pt;color:#000000">学习。不一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.35pt;color:#000000">样</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.22pt;color:#000000">的是，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.61pt;color:#000000">他们可以聚在</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.23pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.62pt;color:#000000">起，输出这样优质的内容</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.06pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.65pt;color:#000000">他们对技术的追求，他们共同的性格特质，也许更值得你体</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.00pt;color:#000000">会。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.12pt;color:#000000">如</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.53pt;color:#000000">果看完本书，你能</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.49pt;color:#000000">够在技术理念上有进</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">步的思考，那肯定比看</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.44pt;color:#000000">本书本身收</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.67pt;color:#000000">获更大。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.54pt;color:#000000">“其实天下之大，又何止南北？勉强求全等于故步自封，</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.47pt;color:#000000">在</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">你眼中这块饼</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.06pt;color:#000000">是一个武林，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.49pt;color:#000000">对我来讲是</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.22pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.34pt;color:#000000">个世界。所谓大成若缺，有缺憾才能有进步，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.33pt;color:#000000">真管</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.28pt;color:#000000">用的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.22pt;color:#000000">话</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.07pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.37pt;color:#000000">南拳又</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">何</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.30pt;color:#000000">止北传</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.40pt;color:#000000">呢？”</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.73pt;color:#000000">我在叶先生出生的佛山旁边一－</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.47pt;color:#000000">广</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.69pt;color:#000000">州，脑海中不断回响</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.47pt;color:#000000">着</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.59pt;color:#000000">这段</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.04pt;color:#000000">话。</span>

<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:10.10pt;color:#000000">IV </span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.47pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.24pt;color:#000000">乐</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.47pt;color:#000000">环</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.64pt;color:#000000">信首</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.67pt;color:#000000">席架构师</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.53pt;color:#000000">兼云</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.59pt;color:#000000">通讯</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.36pt;color:#000000">事</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.47pt;color:#000000">业</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.53pt;color:#000000">部总经理</span>

## Page 8

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:19.39pt;color:#000000">推荐序</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:13.94pt;color:#000000">2</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.63pt;color:#000000">如果去问架构师什么是架构，可能会得到很多不同的答案，每个架构师对“架构”都</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.52pt;color:#000000">有着不一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.64pt;color:#000000">样的理解，当然这不分对错，数据架构、应用架构、物理架构、组织架构等都是</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.76pt;color:#000000">架构，甚至</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.90pt;color:#000000">不仅在计算机行业，各行各业也都会有类似的角色，但我觉得有一个核心的概</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.50pt;color:#000000">念是共</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.63pt;color:#000000">通的：架构必定是在长期的生产活动中，经过人类深度思考，积累下来的最佳实践</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.46pt;color:#000000">和可复</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.54pt;color:#000000">用的合理抽象</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.26pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.42pt;color:#000000">作为</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.10pt;color:#000000">Tim</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.74pt;color:#000000"> 叔的朋友，我也是他发起的高可用架构微信群的早期成员之一，看着高可用</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">架构群一步步发展</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.64pt;color:#000000">起来，聚集了</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.36pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.64pt;color:#000000">大批</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.36pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.78pt;color:#000000">线的互联网架构师一起探讨和交流技术和架构上</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.67pt;color:#000000">的问题。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.62pt;color:#000000">同时这个群也是国内最早的一批尝试“在线群分享”这种形式的微信群，过去技</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.63pt;color:#000000">术会议</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.42pt;color:#000000">的分</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.59pt;color:#000000">享受</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.76pt;color:#000000">限于时间和空间，却在这种形式下变得更加灵活和轻量，同时也能更好地</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.42pt;color:#000000">沉淀下</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.35pt;color:#000000">来</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.23pt;color:#000000">。这里</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.53pt;color:#000000">不得不提到</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.05pt;color:#000000">Tim</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.60pt;color:#000000"> 叔其人，虽然我不清楚技术群分享这个形式是否为</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.00pt;color:#000000">Tim</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.35pt;color:#000000"> 独</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.59pt;color:#000000">创，但</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.55pt;color:#000000">的确是非常“</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.10pt;color:#000000"> Tim</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.59pt;color:#000000">咽</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.10pt;color:#000000">h</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.24pt;color:#000000">”的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.36pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.94pt;color:#000000">个形式。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.15pt;color:#000000">Tim</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.75pt;color:#000000"> 是国内最早的分布式系统和高可用架构的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.42pt;color:#000000">实践者</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.35pt;color:#000000">之一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.39pt;color:#000000">，同时也是</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.35pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.57pt;color:#000000">名活跃的技术</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.53pt;color:#000000">Blogger</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.44pt;color:#000000">。我大概从</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.73pt;color:#000000">2009</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.53pt;color:#000000"> 年开始订阅</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.05pt;color:#000000">Tim</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.46pt;color:#000000"> 叔的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.65pt;color:#000000">Blog</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.54pt;color:#000000">（</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.53pt;color:#000000">后端</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.57pt;color:#000000">技术），上面有很多很有价值和深度的技术文章，我也算是看着</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.15pt;color:#000000">Tim</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.53pt;color:#000000"> 叔的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.74pt;color:#000000">Blog</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.66pt;color:#000000"> 成长起</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.53pt;color:#000000">来的程序员。互</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.61pt;color:#000000">联网的分享精神，在这里就是</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.23pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.63pt;color:#000000">个很好的体现</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.26pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.60pt;color:#000000">随着近几年国内的互联网</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.62pt;color:#000000">蓬勃发展</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.63pt;color:#000000">，新技术层出不穷，行业内也涌现出了很多优秀的工程师和架构师。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.10pt;color:#000000">Tim</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 这两年</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.50pt;color:#000000">就聚集</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.52pt;color:#000000">起这样的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.23pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.57pt;color:#000000">拨人，创造起</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.35pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.65pt;color:#000000">个平台，能让大家的经验互相分享，思想互相碰撞，这</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.38pt;color:#000000">本书就是一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.44pt;color:#000000">个很棒的阶段性产物</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.99pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.46pt;color:#000000">在一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.88pt;color:#000000">名</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.46pt;color:#000000">工程</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.63pt;color:#000000">师的成长过程中，是否培养出“大局观”是</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.35pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.65pt;color:#000000">个重要的转折点。而快速提</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.59pt;color:#000000">升自己</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.47pt;color:#000000">“大局观”的方法之</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.36pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.78pt;color:#000000">就是多观察别人是怎么做的，并从中分析优势和劣势，在你</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.46pt;color:#000000">面对不</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.60pt;color:#000000">同的选择时多看看别人的思考过程，见多必然识广，也许此时你并不能直接解决自</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">己遇</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.88pt;color:#000000">到的问题，但更重要的是吸取别人的经验，思考更全面。这几年随着互联网以及移动</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.35pt;color:#000000">互联网</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.51pt;color:#000000">的爆发，后端技术迭代的速度很快，新技术层见叠出：从</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.00pt;color:#000000">RDBMS</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.12pt;color:#000000"> 到</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.61pt;color:#000000">NoSQL</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.54pt;color:#000000"> 再到最</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.46pt;color:#000000">近的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.26pt;color:#000000">N</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.23pt;color:#000000">ew</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.54pt;color:#000000">SQL</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.37pt;color:#000000">；从单模块到</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.44pt;color:#000000">SO</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.00pt;color:#000000">A</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.54pt;color:#000000"> 再到微服务：从简单的脚本部署和简单的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.00pt;color:#000000">HA</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.35pt;color:#000000"> 到容</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.39pt;color:#000000">器化的</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.62pt;color:#000000">具，该如何做出选择？本书不会明确告诉你答案，但是会通过一篇篇实际案例和分享来拓</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.64pt;color:#000000">展你的眼界和视野，在你面临选择的时候能给到你一些启发。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.62pt;color:#000000">本书并不是面向编程初学者的书，涉及了</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.46pt;color:#000000">一些</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.54pt;color:#000000">比较深的内容，覆盖面也很</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.23pt;color:#000000">广</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.13pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.50pt;color:#000000">建议有</span>

## Page 10

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:19.39pt;color:#000000">推荐序</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:13.79pt;color:#000000">3</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.45pt;color:#000000">我开始以为这是从理论开始的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.22pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.52pt;color:#000000">本讲高可用的书，结果我拿到电子稿后发现</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.22pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.41pt;color:#000000">开始就</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.62pt;color:#000000">是很多不同公司的具体高可用的架构案例，而且是精选过的案例。从案</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.76pt;color:#000000">例切入，</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.63pt;color:#000000">会更加直</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.76pt;color:#000000">接直观地让读者去了解高可用的架构，并且也提供了非常好的可参考的实例，如果读者在</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.52pt;color:#000000">自己的场景中遇到类似问题，可以直接参考。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.51pt;color:#000000">除具体案例外，本书还通过不同公司中系统的设计、改造的经验来介绍高可用的原理</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.62pt;color:#000000">和分布式的实践。这个做法也比较有特色，依然选择了从具体的实践经验和具体的实例出</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.50pt;color:#000000">发，没有去凭空介绍很多道理，实践性非常强，井且案例所涵盖的范围是非常广泛的，和</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.23pt;color:#000000">第</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.26pt;color:#000000">1</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.62pt;color:#000000"> 章的案例精选一样，都来自众多公司的实践。结束了前两章对高可用架构的案例和原</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.38pt;color:#000000">理的介绍后，第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.11pt;color:#000000">3</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000"> 章以电商架构作为一个专题点进行了展开</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.30pt;color:#000000">，在体</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.22pt;color:#000000">量</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.39pt;color:#000000">比较大的时候，利用</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.58pt;color:#000000">电商的后端架构解决高可用还是有比较大的挑战的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.38pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.64pt;color:#000000">一些电商的经验还可以移植或者转化</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.39pt;color:#000000">到别的系统当中，比较有参考价值。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.23pt;color:#000000">第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.85pt;color:#000000">4</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.60pt;color:#000000"> 章从容器和云计算切入，这对高可用来说是</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.35pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.63pt;color:#000000">个重要的基础设施，不论基于公有</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.60pt;color:#000000">云还</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.88pt;color:#000000">是自己在内部做私有云抑或是采用混合云，云都是现在后端绕不过去的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.60pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.87pt;color:#000000">个话题，而</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.64pt;color:#000000">说到容器，就等同于说到了</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.83pt;color:#000000">Docker</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.51pt;color:#000000">，其轻</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.47pt;color:#000000">量</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.72pt;color:#000000">化以及通过</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.84pt;color:#000000">Image</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.75pt;color:#000000"> 来快速部署应用的特点，也</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.47pt;color:#000000">使</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.40pt;color:#000000">Do</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.36pt;color:#000000">cker</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.69pt;color:#000000"> 得到了广泛应用。有了容器和云的支撑</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，那么如何在自身运维保障上能够适配</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.36pt;color:#000000">高</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.65pt;color:#000000">可用的要求，则是第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.28pt;color:#000000">5</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000"> 章的内容。没有高效的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.74pt;color:#000000">、自动的、可靠的运维支撑，是很难保障我</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.23pt;color:#000000">们系统的高可用的。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.77pt;color:#000000">接下来就到了大数据与数据库的部分，做高可用也好，做水平扩展也好，有状态的节</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.18pt;color:#000000">点总</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.64pt;color:#000000">是最难处理的，这个章节专门针对数据库层面去做了案例的分析，大数据本身不仅仅</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:10.60pt;color:#000000">包括了状态，还包括了计算，而大数据的计算往往是单个任务</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:10.57pt;color:#000000">比较重的，那么做到高可用</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.73pt;color:#000000">的挑战和处理我们很多前台的并发更高但是处理时长短、消耗资源</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.76pt;color:#000000">小的并发任务有很大不</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:10.39pt;color:#000000">同，这也是第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.20pt;color:#000000">6</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:10.60pt;color:#000000"> 章会介绍的内容。最后一章，介绍的是安全和网工，这</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:10.62pt;color:#000000">个部分本身为整体</span>

![](./高可用架构（第1卷） (高可用架构社区) (Z-Library)_assets/images/p010_img01.jpg)

---

## Page 11

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.89pt;color:#000000">高可用架构（第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.80pt;color:#000000">1</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.80pt;color:#000000"> 卷）</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">应用系统提供了安全的防护和保障，进而使得从用户层面看系统是可用的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.99pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.76pt;color:#000000">本书的章节设置、前后的逻辑性很强，特别让我赞叹的是全书所有章节都是具体的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.36pt;color:#000000">案</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.50pt;color:#000000">例，没有大套的理论</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.19pt;color:#000000">、</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.33pt;color:#000000">空洞的说教，均从具体实际案例出发来介绍，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.42pt;color:#000000">方面会带给</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.41pt;color:#000000">读者更</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.63pt;color:#000000">强的现场感，另一方面一个个具体的案例都是读者可参考的，相信这本书会给读者</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.54pt;color:#000000">在高可</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.31pt;color:#000000">用架构方面带来更多的信息和收获。</span>

<span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:10.10pt;color:#000000">VIII </span>

## Page 12

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:19.42pt;color:#000000">推荐序</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:14.25pt;color:#000000">4</span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.57pt;color:#000000">记得我还在新浪工作的那会儿，作为</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.23pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.61pt;color:#000000">名职场工程师新人，很早就开始关注</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.00pt;color:#000000">Tim</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.35pt;color:#000000"> 的技</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.57pt;color:#000000">术博客。在理想国际大厦里也常见到</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.05pt;color:#000000">Tim</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.46pt;color:#000000">，但那时</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.30pt;color:#000000">T</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.85pt;color:#000000">im</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.63pt;color:#000000"> 对我来说是“只可远观而不可亵玩</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">焉</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.28pt;color:#000000">”</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.99pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.60pt;color:#000000">很多年过去，随着自己在技术上的成长，我有幸加入到</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.05pt;color:#000000">Tim</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.50pt;color:#000000"> 组织的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.22pt;color:#000000">高可用架构群里。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">高</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.78pt;color:#000000">可用架构群里的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.72pt;color:#000000">项基本规则就是：大家要积极做技术分享。当时作为相对年轻的成员，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.75pt;color:#000000">我有些焦虑，毕竟与群里的大拿比较，我做的事情似乎不够高大上。但在百度完成</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.36pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">段抢</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.39pt;color:#000000">购类</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.47pt;color:#000000">型项目后，我发现在项目中总有些值得提炼的技术可以分享，于是主动联系了</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.96pt;color:#000000">Tim</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000"> 并</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.23pt;color:#000000">表</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.54pt;color:#000000">达了分享的意愿</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.26pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.59pt;color:#000000">让人意外的是，在</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.05pt;color:#000000">Tim</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.62pt;color:#000000"> 事先了解内容的情况下，我也顺利</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.46pt;color:#000000">地</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.42pt;color:#000000">完成了</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.23pt;color:#000000">一</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.73pt;color:#000000">场人气爆棚的群内技术分享，总体反馈是</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.20pt;color:#000000">：效果不错！</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.59pt;color:#000000">事后</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.68pt;color:#000000">也的确有同</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.72pt;color:#000000">学联系我，采用了</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.35pt;color:#000000">我的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.23pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.61pt;color:#000000">些思路在公司内实现了抢购方案，同样</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.52pt;color:#000000">，我也从</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.57pt;color:#000000">高可用架构</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.88pt;color:#000000">的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.35pt;color:#000000">其</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.57pt;color:#000000">他分</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.63pt;color:#000000">享里升华了技</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.58pt;color:#000000">术视野，自此，我感受到了技术交流的重要性。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.62pt;color:#000000">近两年我参加了不少技术会议，翻译了技术书籍，也随着团</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.12pt;color:#000000">队内</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.30pt;color:#000000">不少同学尝试图文、</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.86pt;color:#000000">现场的技术交流，能明显感受到技术社区的活跃</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.87pt;color:#000000">以</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.89pt;color:#000000">及中国技术的快速崛起。当得知高可用</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.36pt;color:#000000">架</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.69pt;color:#000000">构社区要与博文视点联合出品《高可用架构（第</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.91pt;color:#000000">1</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.49pt;color:#000000"> 卷〉》一书时，我强烈支持</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.53pt;color:#000000">，能够让</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.47pt;color:#000000">更</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.00pt;color:#000000">多</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.72pt;color:#000000">的人学习到高可用组织这几年的积累，这是让人兴奋的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.64pt;color:#000000">！虽然本书中我分</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.78pt;color:#000000">享的部分己经</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.23pt;color:#000000">是</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.63pt;color:#000000">两年前的方案，但现在看来，其中的设计思想与问题思考依然有参考价值。在得到博文</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">视</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.12pt;color:#000000">点</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.88pt;color:#000000">送来的样书时，我又重新阅读了书中一些大拿的技术分享，反</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.89pt;color:#000000">倒相比之前通过</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.75pt;color:#000000">手机阅</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.12pt;color:#000000">读</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.28pt;color:#000000">文章有了更多的收获！</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.96pt;color:#000000">所以，这本书，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">定可以作为你技术进阶路上常伴左右的好书</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:3.81pt;color:#000000">！</span>

## Page 14

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.80pt;color:#000000">目</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.82pt;color:#000000">IJ</span><span style="font-family:'Helvetica';font-size:11.19pt;color:#000000"> 1§1 </span>

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.22pt;color:#000000">成为</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.51pt;color:#000000">名优秀的架构师需要哪些条件？首先需要有扎实的编程理论基础，对软件运作</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.56pt;color:#000000">的原理以及算法有深入的理解</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.13pt;color:#000000">：</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.65pt;color:#000000">其次还需要有丰富的实践，能够将理论与实际相结合。除</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.76pt;color:#000000">此之外，从他人优秀的实践经验中学习，是成为卓越架构师最有效的方法。笔者在刚开发</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.35pt;color:#000000">微</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.59pt;color:#000000">博之初，国内并没有类似社交网络的技术经验</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.38pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.93pt;color:#000000">但在国外，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.57pt;color:#000000">Face</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.81pt;color:#000000">book</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.26pt;color:#000000"> 、</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.17pt;color:#000000">Twitter</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.57pt;color:#000000"> 等公司的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.53pt;color:#000000">工程</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.75pt;color:#000000">师发表的相关实践文章，给了笔者所在团队架构师很多启发，团队</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">也顺利地搭建了</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:7.69pt;color:#000000">自</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.88pt;color:#000000">己</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.53pt;color:#000000">的架构，成功应对了业务的飞速增长。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.73pt;color:#000000">搭建高并发及高可用大型系统长期都是业界难题</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.18pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.28pt;color:#000000">Twitter</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.75pt;color:#000000"> 在创建之初，也多次出现不</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.50pt;color:#000000">稳定甚</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.55pt;color:#000000">至岩机的现象</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.06pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.61pt;color:#000000">不少架构师可能有同感</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.13pt;color:#000000">，</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.62pt;color:#000000">大型系统中任何一个小</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.20pt;color:#000000">的模块设计不慎，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.59pt;color:#000000">就可</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.68pt;color:#000000">能会导致部分用户访问失败，甚至全站不能访问的后果</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.59pt;color:#000000">，给用户体验带来</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.16pt;color:#000000">巨大的伤害。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.64pt;color:#000000">因</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.62pt;color:#000000">此在微博核心系统中，团队中的架构师将系统可用性作为设计</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.61pt;color:#000000">的首要考虑因素，如履</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.23pt;color:#000000">薄</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.55pt;color:#000000">冰，一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.73pt;color:#000000">路走来，终于在可用性方面跟同类产品相</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">比取得了更好的成绩</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.47pt;color:#000000">。类</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.75pt;color:#000000">似的，系统可用</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.36pt;color:#000000">性</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.73pt;color:#000000">也应该是大部分互联网系统架构最基本的要求</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.70pt;color:#000000">，这也是笔者发起及</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.75pt;color:#000000">参与高可用架构社区</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">的原</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.52pt;color:#000000">因</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.99pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.74pt;color:#000000">系统的可用性在过去、现在以及未来都是架构领域最重要的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.47pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.75pt;color:#000000">个环节，但是相</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.47pt;color:#000000">关</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.42pt;color:#000000">的知</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.33pt;color:#000000">识并</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">没有太多现成的渠道可以获取。物以类聚，人以群分</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.32pt;color:#000000">，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.39pt;color:#000000">高可用架</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.48pt;color:#000000">构技术社区聚集了业</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.55pt;color:#000000">界关注</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.73pt;color:#000000">互联网架构的人群，并将各大</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.47pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.78pt;color:#000000">线公司具有丰富经验的架构师在社区的分享沉淀成</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.35pt;color:#000000">本</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.51pt;color:#000000">书中的文章</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.26pt;color:#000000">。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.64pt;color:#000000">此外社区也举办全国各地架构主题的技术沙龙、每年一度的全球互联网架</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.36pt;color:#000000">构大</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.30pt;color:#000000">会（</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.45pt;color:#000000">thegiac.com</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.78pt;color:#000000">）以及以高并发为主题的编程竞赛活动，是学习及了解架构最有效的</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.34pt;color:#000000">圈子。</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.62pt;color:#000000">本书内容是高可用架构社区众多讲师对架构领域内容的一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.65pt;color:#000000">个阶段总结，也是社区长</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.28pt;color:#000000">期活</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.22pt;color:#000000">动的</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000">一</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.30pt;color:#000000">个结晶</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:4.78pt;color:#000000">。</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.62pt;color:#000000">带给我们架构方面启发的未必需要长篇大论，像上面提</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.62pt;color:#000000">到的各种形式的偏重实践的架</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.74pt;color:#000000">构总结与思考的文章，往往会带给我们更多帮助。无</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.77pt;color:#000000">独有偶，短小的技术启迪文</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.73pt;color:#000000">章在历史</span>

![](./高可用架构（第1卷） (高可用架构社区) (Z-Library)_assets/images/p014_img01.jpg)

## Page 15

<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.91pt;color:#000000">高可用架构（第</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:5.61pt;color:#000000">1</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.80pt;color:#000000"> 卷）</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.34pt;color:#000000">上也广受欢迎，笔者喜欢的《编程珠矶》一书中就提到，</span>
<span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.19pt;color:#000000">Jo</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.60pt;color:#000000">n</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:6.28pt;color:#000000"> Bentley</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.11pt;color:#000000"> 在《</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:8.19pt;color:#000000">ACM</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.33pt;color:#000000"> 通讯</span><span style="font-family:'HiddenHorzOCR';font-size:9.15pt;color:#000000">》发表</span>

<span style="font-family:'Times-Roman';font-size:8.60pt;color:#000000">1.2.3 </span>
